</p>

</p>

<ol><li>ridiculous, laughable</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***best.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:best.html>best</a> (345)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:best.html>best</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*betst</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*batistaz</i>, superlative of <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*gōdaz</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds"><a href = vnd.unilang:best.html>best</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:best.html>best</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy"><a href = vnd.unilang:best.html>best</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:besten.html>besten</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">bedst</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_2">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:best.html>best</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">Superlative form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:goed.html>goed</a></i></span>; <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:best.html>best</a></span>.</li>
<li>fine, <a href = vnd.unilang:okay.html>okay</a>
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:mag.html>Mag</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:buiten.html>buiten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:spelen.html>spelen</a>?  |  <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vind.html>vind</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:best.html>best</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eten.html>eten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:weer.html>weer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:thuis.html>thuis</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bent.html>bent</a>.</i>
<dl><dd>May I go and play outside?  |  It's <b>fine</b> with <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a>, as long as you're back home again before dinner.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bestaen</i>. <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bestand.html>bestand</a> (5165)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bestant</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">be-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">stand</i>, compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:bestand.html>Bestand</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bestand.html>bestand</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bestanden.html>bestanden</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bestandje.html>bestandje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>archive, file</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">computing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> file</li>
<li>truce

<ol><li>capable of withstanding, capable to withstand

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bestek.html>bestek</a> (14758)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Besteck</i>.

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">besteken</i>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bestek.html>bestek</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bestekken.html>bestekken</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bestek.html>bestekje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p>[A] <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bestek.html>bestek</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic"><a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a></span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bestellen.html>bestellen</a> (3226)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:bestellen.html>bestellen</a></i>. </p>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bestellen.html>bestellen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to order, demand delivery
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wil.html>Wil</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:koffie.html>koffie</a>? <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zal.html>zal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ons.html>ons</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>wat</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bestellen.html>bestellen</a></b>!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Do you want coffee? I will <b>order</b> us some!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to deliver
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>Die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bakkerij.html>bakkerij</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bestelt.html>bestelt</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:nog.html>nog</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:huis.html>huis</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">That bakery still <b>delivers</b> at home.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:bestoken.html>bestoken</a></i>.
